       <article class="post-16690 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-beauty category-giveaway" id="post-16690">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          <a href="http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/" rel="bookmark" title="Permalink to Glitter, Inc. Giveaway No. 5: BIRCHBOX Subscription">
           Glitter, Inc. Giveaway No. 5: BIRCHBOX Subscription
          </a>
         </h1>
         <span class="entry-info">
          By Lexi
          <span class="divider">
           |
          </span>
          September 17, 2013
         </span>
         <div class="sharing">
          <span>
           SHARE THIS POST:
          </span>
          <a href="http://twitter.com/share?&amp;url=http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/" id="tweet-this" target="_blank">
           <img alt="Tweet This" src="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/themes/glitterinc/images/post-tweet.png"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/share.php?u=http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/" id="post-facebook">
           <img alt="Share on Facebook" src="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/themes/glitterinc/images/post-fb.png"/>
          </a>
          <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/" id="gplus-this" target="_blank">
           <img alt="share on Google+" src="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/themes/glitterinc/images/post-gplus.png"/>
          </a>
          <a href="javascript:void((function(){var%20e=document.createElement('script');e.setAttribute('type','text/javascript');e.setAttribute('charset','UTF-8');e.setAttribute('src','http://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinmarklet.js?r='+Math.random()*99999999);document.body.appendChild(e)})());" id="pin-it">
           <img alt="Pin It" src="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/themes/glitterinc/images/post-pin.png"/>
          </a>
          <a href="http://www.stumbleupon.com/submit?url=http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/" id="stumble" target="_blank">

          </a>
          <a href="mailto:?body=I thought you might enjoy this post: Glitter, Inc. Giveaway No. 5: BIRCHBOX Subscription, http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/" id="email-this">
           <img alt="email this post" src="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/themes/glitterinc/images/post-email.png"/>
          </a>
          <div class="right">
           <span class="comments-link">
            <a href="http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/#respond">
             <span class="leave-reply">

             </span>
            </a>
           </span>

        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          Last month, I got the chance to get all dolled up by
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Birchbox
          </a>
          <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://ad.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/show?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;bids=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0" width="1"/>
          for
          <a href="http://glitterinc.com/2013/08/behind-the-scenes-birchbox-ann-taylor/" target="_blank">
           a photo shoot featuring Ann Taylors brand new Fall shoe line
          </a>
          , and then last week
          <a href="http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/new-york-fashion-week-part-2/" target="_blank">
           during New York Fashion Week
          </a>
          , I took a trip to Birchbox Local at Milk Studios. Basically, Im
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Birchbox
          </a>
          <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://ad.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/show?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;bids=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0" width="1"/>
          -obsessed. And you should be too. Which is why, thanks to
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Birchbox
          </a>
          <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://ad.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/show?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;bids=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0" width="1"/>
          , were giving one lucky reader a Birchbox Subscription!
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/birchbox-style-subscription-giveaway-beauty-_-glitterinc.com_.png" rel="attachment wp-att-16692">
           <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
            <img alt="birchbox style subscription giveaway beauty _ glitterinc.com" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-16692" height="405" src="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/birchbox-style-subscription-giveaway-beauty-_-glitterinc.com_.png" width="660"/>
            <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://glitterinc.com/2013/09/glitter-inc-giveaway-3-birchbox-subscription/&amp;media=http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/birchbox-style-subscription-giveaway-beauty-_-glitterinc.com_.png&amp;description=Glitter, Inc. Giveaway No. 5: BIRCHBOX Subscription')">
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          For beauty-box-newbies:
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Birchbox
          </a>
          sends a dream beauty care package each month as part of their subscription-based service. Each month, you receive a selection of samples and full-sized items that the
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Birchbox
          </a>
          Editors have tried (and retried) themselves. They scout their samples from both well-known brands and emerging gems. The womens subscription includes everything from skincare to makeup, as well as some fun non-beauty extras.
         </p>
         <p>
          Enter to win one 3-month subscription to
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Birchbox
          </a>
          using the Rafflecopter below  (please complete all entries; following on Instagram and/or tweeting about the giveaway is optional.)
         </p>
         <p>
          <a class="rafl" href="http://www.rafflecopter.com/rafl/display/d953b05/" id="rc-d953b05" rel="nofollow">
           a Rafflecopter giveaway
          </a>
          <br/>
          <script src="//d12vno17mo87cx.cloudfront.net/embed/rafl/cptr.js" type="text/javascript">
          </script>
         </p>
         <p>
          And in case you dont win this one,
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Skip the Line and get yourself a Birchbox subscription!
          </a>
          <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://ad.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/show?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;bids=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0" width="1"/>
          <strong>
          </strong>
           Im so excited to offer all of my readers a skip the line opportunity at Birchbox! Instead of a 4-week wait (Birchbox is
          <em>
           that
          </em>
          popular!), if you subscribe through Glitter, Inc. youll be able to instantly purchase a subscription to Birchbox. (Just click here:
          <a href="http://click.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/click?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;offerid=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0">
           Join Birchbox!
          </a>
          <img alt="" border="0" height="1" src="http://ad.linksynergy.com/fs-bin/show?id=7NYHSplM6vY&amp;bids=300463.70&amp;type=3&amp;subid=0" width="1"/>
          )
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Good Luck!
          </em>
          <em>
           Entries will be accepted through 12AM EST on Friday,
           <strong>
            September 27th, 2013.
           </strong>
           One winner will be chosen at random through Rafflecopter.
           <em>
            Open to US Residents only. Please note entries will be verified.
           </em>
           The winner will be notified by email via lexi@glitterinc.com. The winner will have 48 hours to respond or a new winner will be chosen.
           <br/>
          </em>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           No purchase necessary; void where prohibited.
          </em>
          <em>
           By entering into this sweepstakes, the entrant acknowledges that they are eligible for this sweepstakes according to all laws set forth by their state of residency.
          </em>
         </p>
         <br/>
         <img alt="Lexi" src="http://glitterinc.com/wp-content/themes/glitterinc/images/lexi-signature.png"/>
        </div>

                                        fields[2] = {'value':1970};//trick birthdays into having years
                                    }
                                	if ( fields[0].value=='MM' &amp;&amp; fields[1].value=='DD' &amp;&amp; (fields[2].value=='YYYY' || (bday &amp;&amp; fields[2].value==1970) ) ){
                                		this.value = '';
								    } else if ( fields[0].value=='' &amp;&amp; fields[1].value=='' &amp;&amp; (fields[2].value=='' || (bday &amp;&amp; fields[2].value==1970) ) ){
                                		this.value = '';
								    } else {
								        if (/\[day\]/.test(fields[0].name)){
	                                        this.value = fields[1].value+'/'+fields[0].value+'/'+fields[2].value;									        
								        } else {
	                                        this.value = fields[0].value+'/'+fields[1].value+'/'+fields[2].value;
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                        });
                    return mce_validator.form();
                }, 
                success: mce_success_cb
            };
  $('#mc-embedded-subscribe-form').ajaxForm(options);
   
});
function mce_success_cb(resp){
	jQuery(document).ready( function($) {
    $('#mce-success-response').hide();
    $('#mce-error-response').hide();
    if (resp.result=="success"){
        $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
        $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html('Thank you! Please check your email to confirm your subscription.');
        $('#mc-embedded-subscribe-form').each(function(){
            this.reset();
    	}).hide();
    } else {
        var index = -1;
        var msg;
        try {
            var parts = resp.msg.split(' - ',2);
            if (parts[1]==undefined){
                msg = resp.msg;
            } else {
                i = parseInt(parts[0]);
                if (i.toString() == parts[0]){
                    index = parts[0];
                    msg = parts[1];
                } else {
                    index = -1;
                    msg = resp.msg;
                }
            }
        } catch(e){
            index = -1;
            msg = resp.msg;
        }
        try{
            if (index== -1){
                $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
                $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html(msg);            
            } else {
                err_id = 'mce_tmp_error_msg';
                html = '&lt;div id="'+err_id+'" style="'+err_style+'"&gt; '+msg+'&lt;/div&gt;';
                
                var input_id = '#mc_embed_signup';
                var f = $(input_id);
                if (ftypes[index]=='address'){
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index]+'-addr1';
                    f = $(input_id).parent().parent().get(0);
                } else if (ftypes[index]=='date'){
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index]+'-month';
                    f = $(input_id).parent().parent().get(0);
                } else {
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index];
                    f = $().parent(input_id).get(0);
                }
                if (f){
                    $(f).append(html);
                    $(input_id).focus();
                } else {
                    $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
                    $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html(msg);
                }
            }
        } catch(e){
            $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').show();
            $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response').html(msg);
        }
    }
	});
}
var fnames = new Array();var ftypes = new Array();fnames[0]='EMAIL';ftypes[0]='email';fnames[1]='FNAME';ftypes[1]='text';fnames[2]='LNAME';ftypes[2]='text';
 
jQuery(document).ready( function($) {
  var options = { errorClass: 'mce_inline_error', errorElement: 'div', onkeyup: function(){}, onfocusout:function(){}, onblur:function(){}  };
  var mce_validator = $("#mc-embedded-subscribe-form2").validate(options);
  $("#mc-embedded-subscribe-form2").unbind('submit');//remove the validator so we can get into beforeSubmit on the ajaxform, which then calls the validator
  options = { url: 'http://glitterandpearls.us5.list-manage.com/subscribe/post-json?u=d6f64de2f85afebc123eade6c&amp;id=3e4762dfc5&amp;c=?', type: 'GET', dataType: 'json', contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                beforeSubmit: function(){
                    $('#mce_tmp_error_msg2').remove();
                    $('.datefield','#mc_embed_signup2').each(
                        function(){
                            var txt = 'filled';
                            var fields = new Array();
                            var i = 0;
                            $(':text', this).each(
                                function(){
                                    fields[i] = this;
                                    i++;
                                });
                            $(':hidden', this).each(
                                function(){
                                    var bday = false;
                                    if (fields.length == 2){
                                        bday = true;
                                        fields[2] = {'value':1970};//trick birthdays into having years
                                    }
                                	if ( fields[0].value=='MM' &amp;&amp; fields[1].value=='DD' &amp;&amp; (fields[2].value=='YYYY' || (bday &amp;&amp; fields[2].value==1970) ) ){
                                		this.value = '';
								    } else if ( fields[0].value=='' &amp;&amp; fields[1].value=='' &amp;&amp; (fields[2].value=='' || (bday &amp;&amp; fields[2].value==1970) ) ){
                                		this.value = '';
								    } else {
								        if (/\[day\]/.test(fields[0].name)){
	                                        this.value = fields[1].value+'/'+fields[0].value+'/'+fields[2].value;									        
								        } else {
	                                        this.value = fields[0].value+'/'+fields[1].value+'/'+fields[2].value;
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                        });
                    return mce_validator.form();
                }, 
                success: mce_success_cb
            };
  $("#mc-embedded-subscribe-form2").ajaxForm(options);
   
});
function mce_success_cb(resp){
	jQuery(document).ready( function($) {
    $('#mce-success-response2').hide();
    $('#mce-error-response2').hide();
    if (resp.result=="success"){
        $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').show();
        $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').html('Thank you! Please check your email to confirm your subscription.');
        $('#mc-embedded-subscribe-form2').each(function(){
            this.reset();
    	}).hide();
    	setTimeout("parent.$.fancybox.close()", 1500);
    } else {
        var index = -1;
        var msg;
        try {
            var parts = resp.msg.split(' - ',2);
            if (parts[1]==undefined){
                msg = resp.msg;
            } else {
                i = parseInt(parts[0]);
                if (i.toString() == parts[0]){
                    index = parts[0];
                    msg = parts[1];
                } else {
                    index = -1;
                    msg = resp.msg;
                }
            }
        } catch(e){
            index = -1;
            msg = resp.msg;
        }
        try{
            if (index== -1){
                $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').show();
                $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').html(msg);            
            } else {
                err_id = 'mce_tmp_error_msg';
                html = '&lt;div id="'+err_id+'2" style="'+err_style+'"&gt; '+msg+'&lt;/div&gt;';
                
                var input_id = '#mc_embed_signup2';
                var f = $(input_id);
                if (ftypes[index]=='address'){
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index]+'-addr1';
                    f = $(input_id).parent().parent().get(0);
                } else if (ftypes[index]=='date'){
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index]+'-month';
                    f = $(input_id).parent().parent().get(0);
                } else {
                    input_id = '#mce-'+fnames[index];
                    f = $().parent(input_id).get(0);
                }
                if (f){
                    $(f).append(html);
                    $(input_id).focus();
                } else {
                    $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').show();
                    $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').html(msg);
                }
            }
        } catch(e){
            $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').show();
            $('#mce-'+resp.result+'-response2').html(msg);
        }
    }
	});
}
